Trigger crown_britain
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

 Condition IsFactionLeader 
 and EndedInSettlement 
 and FactionType england 
 and I_SettlementOwner London = england
 and I_SettlementOwner Nottingham = england
 and I_SettlementOwner York = england
 ;and I_SettlementOwner Exeter = england
 and I_SettlementOwner Winchester = england
 and I_SettlementOwner Caernarvon = england
 and I_SettlementOwner Edinburgh = england
 ;and I_SettlementOwner Aberdeen = england
 and I_SettlementOwner Inverness = england
 and I_SettlementOwner Dublin = england
 and not I_WorldwideAncillaryExists crown_england
 
 AcquireAncillary crown_england chance 100

 and not HasAncType office ;and doesn't have another office

 and not HasAncType office_military2
 
 AcquireAncillary moh_muslim chance 50

;gets assigned without player input- same for AI 
Trigger moh_mongol 
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd 
 Condition IsGeneral
 and not CharFactionType moors
 and not CharFactionType egypt
 and not CharFactionType turks
 and not CharFactionType kwarezm
 and not CharFactionType timurids ;abbasids
 and not CharFactionType portugal ;zirids
 and EndedInSettlement
 and not IsFactionLeader
 and not IsFactionHeir
 and SettlementBuildingExists >= wooden_castle ;so you must have a castle
 and SettlementBuildingExists >= stables
 and Attribute Loyalty >= 6
 and Trait MilitaryInclination >= 1
 and not FactionwideAncillaryExists moh_mongol
 and FactionwideAncillaryExists marshall_mongol ;as the marshall assigns this office
 and not HasAncType office ;and doesn't have another office
 and not HasAncType office_military1
 and not HasAncType office_military2
 
 AcquireAncillary moh_mongol chance 50

 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd 
 Condition CharacterReligion catholic 
 and not I_WorldwideAncillaryExists protector
 and IsFactionLeader
 ;wait until 4th turn so that random numbers are closer to random
 and not FactionExcommunicated

 AcquireAncillary protector chance 5 ;will go around until ONE king gets it.

Trigger banner_of_Great_Constantine
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd
 Condition EndedInSettlement
 and IsFactionLeader
 and SettlementName Constantinople
 and FactionType byzantium 
 and not I_WorldwideAncillaryExists banner_of_Great_Constantine
 and not HasAncType Relic_banner
 and Trait GoodCommander >= 3

 AcquireAncillary banner_of_Great_Constantine chance 33
;----------------------------------------------
Trigger sword_of_Basil_Bulgaroctonos
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd
 Condition EndedInSettlement
 and IsGeneral
 and SettlementName Sofia
 and FactionType byzantium 
 and not I_WorldwideAncillaryExists sword_of_Basil_Bulgaroctonos
 and not HasAncType Relic_sword
 and Trait GoodCommander >= 3

 AcquireAncillary sword_of_Basil_Bulgaroctonos chance 33
;----------------------------------------------
Trigger Banner_of_Herakleios
 WhenToTest PostBattle
 Condition WonBattle
; and FactionReligion catholic
 and GeneralFoughtCulture middle_eastern
 and BattleSuccess = crushing
 and FactionType byzantium 
 and not I_WorldwideAncillaryExists Banner_of_Herakleios
 and not HasAncType Relic_banner
 and Trait GoodCommander >= 3
 
 AcquireAncillary Banner_of_Herakleios chance 66
;----------------------------------------------
Trigger sword_of_Great_Constantine
 WhenToTest PostBattle
 Condition IsGeneral
 and WonBattle
 and PercentageEnemyKilled > 25
 and BattleOdds <= 0.50
 and FactionType byzantium 
 and not I_WorldwideAncillaryExists sword_of_Great_Constantine
 and not HasAncType Relic_sword
 and Trait GoodCommander >= 3

 AcquireAncillary sword_of_Great_Constantine chance 66

 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

 and SettlementName Frankfurt
 and AgentType = priest
 and Trait PriestLevel >= 1
 and FactionIsLocal ;for player only
 and FactionType hre
 and not HasAncType hre_elector1
 and not HasAncType hre_elector2
 and not HasAncType hre_elector3
 and not HasAncType hre_elector4
 and not HasAncType hre_elector5
 and not HasAncType hre_elector6
 and not HasAncType hre_elector7
 and not FactionwideAncillaryExists hre_elector_frankfurt
